route-policy ALL
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy mark
  set community ROUTE-KES additive
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy Deneme
  if destination in Deneme then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy TE_IN_V4
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy TE_OUT_V4
  pass
end-policy
!
route-policy CGNAT-TEST
  if destination in (176.218.160.0/24, 176.217.240.0/24, 176.218.160.0/24) then
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    set local-preference 200
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy Full_Route
  if community matches-any Ulakbim_Ddos then
    drop
  endif
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy PERMIT_ANY
  done
end-policy
!
route-policy IKSV_IMPORT
  delete community all
  if destination in (62.244.235.8/32, 84.44.78.192/28) then
    set local-preference 100
    set weight 0
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy IPv6-BGP-LU
  if destination in PFX-ALL-BGP-IPv6-LU-LOOPBACKS then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy VCNO_GECICI
  #NAT44_VF_BLOCKS_128
  if destination in NAT44_VF_BLOCKS_128 then
    done
  endif
  #NAT44_VF_BLOCKS_46_0_0
  if destination in NAT44_VF_BLOCKS_46_0_0 then
    done
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy ANKARA-M10-2
  if destination in Default then
    set local-preference 80
    done
  endif
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Voice-Customers then
    set community Customer-Voice-Subnetted additive
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy BGP-Customers
  set community BGP-Customers additive
end-policy
!
route-policy Dpi_loop-Test
  delete community all
  if destination in (31.206.240.24/30) then
    set community BGP-Customers additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
!
route-policy ALL_Local_Pref
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any NO-EXPORT-VF then
    set community NO-EXPORT-GLOBAL additive
    pass
  endif
  #PREF_230
  if community matches-any PREF_230 then
    set local-preference 230
    done
  endif
  #PREF_140
  if community matches-any PREF_140 then
    set local-preference 140
    done
  endif
  #PREF_155
  if community matches-any PREF_155 then
    set local-preference 155
    done
  endif
  #PREF_160
  if community matches-any PREF_160 then
    set local-preference 160
    done
  endif
  #PREF_170
  if community matches-any PREF_170 then
    set local-preference 170
    done
  endif
  #PREF_159
  if community matches-any PREF_159 then
    set local-preference 159
    done
  endif
  #PREF_100
  if community matches-any PREF_100 then
    set local-preference 100
    done
  endif
  set local-preference 200
end-policy

  drop

route-policy from_sol_tier1_import_yeni
  delete community all
  #REJECT INVALID RPKI
  if validation-state is invalid then
    drop
  endif
  #REMOVE_RFC1918 
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT_SMALLER_THAN-/24
  if destination in Smaller_Than_24 then
    drop
  endif
  if destination in Default then
    drop
  endif
  #REJECT TT PREFIXES
  if as-path in (ios-regex '9121.*') then
    drop
  endif
  if as-path in ISNET then
    set local-preference 172
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community sol additive
    done
  endif
  if destination in ISG_IP_Transit_Service_Over_SOL then
    set community ISG_SOL_RR_Deny additive
    done
  endif
  #SOL ortak_bgp_musterileri
  if destination in ortak_bgp_musterileri then
    set local-preference 160
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community sol additive
    done
  endif
  #Accept-Route-sol 
  if destination in Accept-Route-sol or as-path in (ios-regex '^34984_') then
    set local-preference 170
    set community tier1_global_community additive
    set community sol additive
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy IPT_GZM1_VCNO_EXPORT_V6_PARENT
  if community matches-any IZMIR_DRC then
    apply DRC_Mobil_IzmirINT-1_BGP_EXPORT
    done
  elseif community matches-any VCNO_IZMIR_INT1_COMMUNITY_SECONDARY then
    prepend as-path 15924 4
    apply IPT_GZM1_VCNO_EXPORT_V6
    done
  elseif community matches-any OTHER_THAN_VCNO_PRIMARY_IZMIR_INT1_COMMUNITY then
    prepend as-path 15924 7
    apply IPT_GZM1_VCNO_EXPORT_V6
    done
  else
    apply IPT_GZM1_VCNO_EXPORT_V6
  endif
  drop
end-policy

route-policy ibgp_export_to_m40e2_inet_to_rr
  #REJECT RFC1918
  if destination in Reject-RFC1918 then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any TT-BLACKHOLE then
    drop
  endif
  #ACCEPT IR PREFIXES
  if community matches-any INTEROUTE then
    done
  endif
  #ACCEPT TNAP PREFIXES
  if community matches-any tier1_global_community then
    done
  endif
  #REJECT TR VOICE BACKBONE FOR EUROPE REDUNDANCY
  if destination in TR_VOICE_BACKBONE then
    drop
  endif
  if community matches-any BGP-Customers then
    set next-hop self
    done
  endif
  if as-path is-local then
    done
  endif
  drop
end-policy
